Section 3 — Class Distribution

Imbalance ratio: 1 fraud per 598 legitimate
Naive accuracy: 99.83% (predict all = legitimate, catch zero fraud)
Accuracy is NOT a valid metric. Need to use F1-score and AUC-PR.
Saved: outputs\figures\01_class_distribution.png

Key Findings

1. Dataset Size
   Total          : 283,726
   Legitimate (0) : 283,253  (99.8333%)
   Fraud      (1) : 473  (0.1667%)
   Missing values : None,    Duplicates removed : 1081

2. Class Imbalance
   Ratio         : 1 fraud per 598 legitimate
   Naive accuracy: 99.83%  (catch zero fraud)
   Use F1-score, AUC-PR, and MCC. Not accuracy.

3. Most Discriminative PCA Features
   Top 5 by mean difference: V14, V3, V17, V12, V10
   Top 3 positive corr with fraud : ['V11', 'V4', 'V2']
   Top 3 negative corr with fraud : ['V17', 'V14', 'V12']

4. Amount
   Fraud mean   : EUR 123.87
   Fraud median : EUR 9.82
   Legit median : EUR 22.00
   Long-tail. log_Amount used in all experiments.

5. Temporal Features
   Peak fraud hour : 2:00  (rate = 1.4510%)
   hour_sin and hour_cos INCLUDED.

6. Veocity Features
   Excluded. Negligible correlation (<0.023). Card IDs anonymised.
